<p class="has-text-align-center"><h1 class="kt-adv-heading615820_2ca0e2-90 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading615820_2ca0e2-90">

<p class="has-text-align-center"><em>Welcome to Family Felicity!</h1>
<p class="has-text-align-center"><em>Happier Moms, Creating Happier Families&#8230;</em></p>
<p class="has-text-align-center">This company was built to inform, encourage, and create a supportive community for mothers, and their families. If you’re ready to add more confidence, knowledge, joy, community, and intention to your days, you’ve come to the right place!</p>
<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column615820_55fc3e-9c inner-column-2"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
